        </a>
        , in Downtown So Paulo.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Urban_planning">
       Urban planning
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=S%C3%A3o_Paulo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Urban planning">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Passeio_de_Helic%C3%B3ptero_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo24.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2198" data-file-width="3135" height="154" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Passeio_de_Helic%C3%B3ptero_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo24.jpg/220px-Passeio_de_Helic%C3%B3ptero_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo24.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Passeio_de_Helic%C3%B3ptero_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo24.jpg/330px-Passeio_de_Helic%C3%B3ptero_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo24.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Passeio_de_Helic%C3%B3ptero_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo24.jpg/440px-Passeio_de_Helic%C3%B3ptero_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo24.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Passeio_de_Helic%C3%B3ptero_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo24.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Changes in urban fabrics in the region of Pacaembu neighborhood: side by side, vertical areas and low houses
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:SP_from_Altino_Arantes_Building.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3264" data-file-width="4912" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/SP_from_Altino_Arantes_Building.jpg/220px-SP_from_Altino_Arantes_Building.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/SP_from_Altino_Arantes_Building.jpg/330px-SP_from_Altino_Arantes_Building.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/SP_from_Altino_Arantes_Building.jpg/440px-SP_from_Altino_Arantes_Building.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:SP_from_Altino_Arantes_Building.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        The city view from
        <a href="/wiki/Altino_Arantes_Building" title="Altino Arantes Building">
         Altino Arantes Building
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:S%C3%A3o_Paulo_view.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="853" data-file-width="1280" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_view.jpg/220px-S%C3%A3o_Paulo_view.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_view.jpg/330px-S%C3%A3o_Paulo_view.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_view.jpg/440px-S%C3%A3o_Paulo_view.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:S%C3%A3o_Paulo_view.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Vale do Anhangaba, in
        <a href="/wiki/Central_Zone_of_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Central Zone of So Paulo">
         Downtown
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      So Paulo has a history of actions, projects and plans related to urban planning that can be traced to the governments of Antonio da Silva Prado, Baron Duprat, Washington and Luis Francisco Prestes Maia. However, in general, the city was formed during the 20th century, growing from village to metropolis through a series of informal processes and irregular urban sprawl.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">
       <a href="#cite_note-97">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        97
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Urban growth in So Paulo has followed three patterns since the beginning of the 20th century, according to several urban historians: since the late 19th Century and until the 1940s, So Paulo was a condensed city in which different social groups lived in a small urban zone separated by type of housing; from the 1940s to the 1980s, So Paulo followed a model of center-periphery social segregation, in which the upper and middle-classes occupied central and modern areas while the poor moved towards precarious, self-built housing in the periphery; and from the 1980s onward, new transformations have brought the social classes closer together in spatial terms, but separated by walls and security technologies that seek to isolate the richer classes in the name of security.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Caldeira.2C_Teresa_P._R._2000._p._215_98-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Caldeira.2C_Teresa_P._R._2000._p._215-98">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        98
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Thus, So Paulo differs considerably from other Brazilian cities such as
      <a href="/wiki/Belo_Horizonte" title="Belo Horizonte">
       Belo Horizonte
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Goi%C3%A2nia" title="Goinia">
       Goinia
      </a>
      , whose initial expansion followed determinations by a plan, or a city like
      <a href="/wiki/Bras%C3%ADlia" title="Braslia">
       Braslia
      </a>
      , whose master plan had been fully developed prior to construction.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">
       <a href="#cite_note-99">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        99
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      The effectiveness of these plans has been seen by some planners and historians as questionable. Some of these scholars argue that such plans were produced exclusively for the benefit of the wealthier strata of the population while the working classes would be relegated to the traditional informal processes. In So Paulo until the mid-1950s, the plans were based on the idea of "demolish and rebuild", including former Mayor Prestes Maia So Paulo's road plan (known as the Avenues Plan) or Saturnino de Brito's plan for the Tiet River.
     </p>
     <p>
      The Plan of the Avenues was implemented during the 1920s and sought to build large avenues connecting the city center with the outskirts. This plan included renewing the commercial city center, leading to real estate speculation and gentrification of several downtown neighborhoods . The plan also led to the expansion of bus services, which would soon replace the trolley as the preliminary transportation system.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">
       <a href="#cite_note-100">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        100
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      This contributed to the outwards expansion of So Paulo and the peripherization of poorer residents. Peripheral neighborhoods were usually unregulated and consisted mainly of self-built single-family houses.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Caldeira.2C_Teresa_P._R._2000._p._215_98-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Caldeira.2C_Teresa_P._R._2000._p._215-98">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        98
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In 1968 the Urban Development Plan proposed the Basic Plan for Integrated Development of So Paulo, under the administration of Figueiredo Ferraz. The main result was zoning laws. It lasted until 2004 when the Basic Plan was replaced by the current Master Plan.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">
       <a href="#cite_note-101">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        101
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      That zoning, adopted in 1972, designated "Z1" areas (
      <a href="/wiki/Residential_area" title="Residential area">
       residential areas
      </a>
      designed for elites) and "Z3" (a "mixed zone" lacking clear definitions about their characteristics). Zoning encouraged the growth of suburbs with minimal control and major speculation.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">
       <a href="#cite_note-102">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        102
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      After the 1970s peripheral lot regulation increased and infrastructure in the periphery improved, driving land prices up. The poorest and the newcomers were now unable to purchase their lot and build their house, and were forced to look for a housing alternative. As a result,
      <a href="/wiki/Favela" title="Favela">
       favelas
      </a>
      and precarious tenements (cortios) appeared.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">
       <a href="#cite_note-103">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        103
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      These housing types were often located closer to the center of the city: favelas could sprawl in any terrain that had not previously been utilized (often dangerous or unsanitary) and decaying or abandoned buildings for tenements were abundant inside the city. Favelas went back into the urban perimeter, occupying the small lots that had not yet been occupied by urbanizationalongside polluted rivers, railways, or between bridges.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">
       <a href="#cite_note-104">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        104
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      By 1993, 19.8% of So Paulos population lived in
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Favelas" title="Favelas">
       favelas
      </a>
      , compared to 5.2% in 1980.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">
       <a href="#cite_note-105">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        105
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Today, 2.1 million Paulistas live in favelas, while this only represents 11% of the total population.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">
       <a href="#cite_note-106">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        106
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <div class="thumb tnone" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right:auto; width:99%; max-width:1408px;">
      <div class="thumbinner">
       <div class="overflowbugx" style="overflow:auto;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Panorama_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo.jpg" title="Panoramic view of the city at night from Ibirapuera Park">
         <img alt="" data-file-height="758" data-file-width="5616" height="189" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Panorama_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo.jpg/1400px-Panorama_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Panorama_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo.jpg/2100px-Panorama_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Panorama_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo.jpg/2800px-Panorama_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo.jpg 2x" width="1400"/>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a href="/wiki/File:Panorama_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo.jpg" title="File:Panorama de So Paulo.jpg">
         </a>
        </div>
        <center>
         Panoramic view of the city at night from
         <a href="/wiki/Ibirapuera_Park" title="Ibirapuera Park">
          Ibirapuera Park
         </a>
        </center>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Education">
       Education
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=S%C3%A3o_Paulo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Education">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">
      Main article:
      <a href="/wiki/Education_in_Brazil" title="Education in Brazil">
       Education in Brazil
      </a>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Faculdade_de_Direito_da_USP.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="800" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Faculdade_de_Direito_da_USP.jpg/220px-Faculdade_de_Direito_da_USP.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Faculdade_de_Direito_da_USP.jpg/330px-Faculdade_de_Direito_da_USP.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Faculdade_de_Direito_da_USP.jpg/440px-Faculdade_de_Direito_da_USP.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Faculdade_de_Direito_da_USP.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/Faculdade_de_Direito_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Faculdade de Direito da Universidade de So Paulo">
         Law School of the University of So Paulo
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mackenzie_-_biblioteca_central_George_Alexander.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="518" data-file-width="691" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Mackenzie_-_biblioteca_central_George_Alexander.jpg/220px-Mackenzie_-_biblioteca_central_George_Alexander.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Mackenzie_-_biblioteca_central_George_Alexander.jpg/330px-Mackenzie_-_biblioteca_central_George_Alexander.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Mackenzie_-_biblioteca_central_George_Alexander.jpg/440px-Mackenzie_-_biblioteca_central_George_Alexander.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mackenzie_-_biblioteca_central_George_Alexander.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        "George Alexander" Central Library at the
        <a href="/wiki/Mackenzie_Presbyterian_University" title="Mackenzie Presbyterian University">
         Mackenzie Presbyterian University
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      So Paulo has a system of public and private primary and secondary schools and a variety of vocational-
      <a href="/wiki/Technical_school" title="Technical school">
       technical schools
      </a>
      . More than nine-tenths of the population are literate and roughly the same proportion of those age 7 to 14 are enrolled in school. There are more than 578 universities in the whole state of So Paulo.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">
       <a href="#cite_note-107">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        107
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Educational_institutions">
       Educational institutions
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=S%C3%A3o_Paulo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Educational institutions">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      The universities and colleges include:
     </p>
     <div class="div-col columns column-count column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2;">
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/University_of_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="University of So Paulo">
         Universidade de So Paulo
        </a>
        (USP) (University of So Paulo);
       </li>
       <li>
        Insper Instituto de Ensino e Pesquisa (Insper-SP) (Insper Institute of Education and Research);
       </li>
       <li>
        INPG Business School;
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Pontif%C3%ADcia_Universidade_Cat%C3%B3lica_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Pontifcia Universidade Catlica de So Paulo">
         Pontifcia Universidade Catlica de So Paulo
        </a>
        (PUC-SP) (Pontifical Catholic University of So Paulo);
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Universidade_Presbiteriana_Mackenzie" title="Universidade Presbiteriana Mackenzie">
         Universidade Presbiteriana Mackenzie
        </a>
        (MACKENZIE-SP) (Mackenzie Presbyterian University)
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Instituto_Federal_de_Educa%C3%A7%C3%A3o,_Ci%C3%AAncia_e_Tecnologia_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Instituto Federal de Educao, Cincia e Tecnologia de So Paulo">
         Instituto Federal de Educao, Cincia e Tecnologia de So Paulo
        </a>
        (IFSP) (So Paulo Federal Institute of Education, Science and Technology);
       </li>

        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Unesp" title="Unesp">

       </li>

        (USJT) (So Judas Tadeu University/"So Judas University");

        </a>

       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Funda%C3%A7%C3%A3o_Get%C3%BAlio_Vargas" title="Fundao Getlio Vargas">

        </a>
        (FGV-SP) (Getlio Vargas Foundation);
       </li>

         Fundao Armando Alvares Penteado
        </a>
        (FAAP) (Armando Alvares Penteado Foundation);
       </li>

        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anhembi_Morumbi" title="Anhembi Morumbi">

       </li>

       </li>

        </a>

        <a href="/wiki/Capital_market" title="Capital market">

        </a>
        Institute);

         Faculdade de Comunicao Social Csper Lbero

        (Csper Lbero

       </li>
