        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Pinacoteca_do_Estado_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Pinacoteca do Estado de So Paulo">
         Pinacotheca of the State of So Paulo
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Memorial_da_Am%C3%A9rica_Latina_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Brasil.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1586" data-file-width="2580" height="135" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Memorial_da_Am%C3%A9rica_Latina_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Brasil.jpg/220px-Memorial_da_Am%C3%A9rica_Latina_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Brasil.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Memorial_da_Am%C3%A9rica_Latina_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Brasil.jpg/330px-Memorial_da_Am%C3%A9rica_Latina_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Brasil.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/Memorial_da_Am%C3%A9rica_Latina_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Brasil.jpg/440px-Memorial_da_Am%C3%A9rica_Latina_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Brasil.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Memorial_da_Am%C3%A9rica_Latina_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Brasil.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Latin_America_Memorial" title="Latin America Memorial">
         Latin America Memorial
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Edifica%C3%A7%C3%A3o_do_Memorial_do_Imigrante_e_seus_Jardins.JPG">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="640" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Edifica%C3%A7%C3%A3o_do_Memorial_do_Imigrante_e_seus_Jardins.JPG/220px-Edifica%C3%A7%C3%A3o_do_Memorial_do_Imigrante_e_seus_Jardins.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Edifica%C3%A7%C3%A3o_do_Memorial_do_Imigrante_e_seus_Jardins.JPG/330px-Edifica%C3%A7%C3%A3o_do_Memorial_do_Imigrante_e_seus_Jardins.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Edifica%C3%A7%C3%A3o_do_Memorial_do_Imigrante_e_seus_Jardins.JPG/440px-Edifica%C3%A7%C3%A3o_do_Memorial_do_Imigrante_e_seus_Jardins.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Edifica%C3%A7%C3%A3o_do_Memorial_do_Imigrante_e_seus_Jardins.JPG" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        The Museum of Immigration,
        <i>
         "Museu da Imigrao"
        </i>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MIS,_SP,_5.JPG">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="800" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/MIS%2C_SP%2C_5.JPG/220px-MIS%2C_SP%2C_5.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/MIS%2C_SP%2C_5.JPG/330px-MIS%2C_SP%2C_5.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/MIS%2C_SP%2C_5.JPG/440px-MIS%2C_SP%2C_5.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MIS,_SP,_5.JPG" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Museum_of_Image_and_Sound" title="So Paulo Museum of Image and Sound">
         So Paulo Museum of Image and Sound
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      To be part of the political and economic history of Brazil, So Paulo is practically a museum in the open sky, with neighborhoods and buildings of incalculable historical value. The city has a huge variety of museums and art galleries, which have collections of various styles, from modern religious art, and facts about science, politics, religion, among others. Among the most famous museums in the city are
      <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Museum_of_Art" title="So Paulo Museum of Art">
       So Paulo Museum of Art
      </a>
      (MASP), the
      <a href="/wiki/Museu_Paulista" title="Museu Paulista">
       Ipiranga Museum
      </a>
      , the Museum of Sacred Art, the
      <a href="/wiki/Museum_of_the_Portuguese_Language" title="Museum of the Portuguese Language">
       Museum of the Portuguese Language
      </a>
      , the
      <a href="/wiki/Pinacoteca_do_Estado_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Pinacoteca do Estado de So Paulo">
       Pinacoteca do Estado de So Paulo
      </a>
      , among other renowned institutions. It also houses one of the top five zoos in the world, the
      <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Zoo" title="So Paulo Zoo">
       So Paulo Zoo
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">
       <a href="#cite_note-138">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        138
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Popularly known as "Ipiranga Museum", the first monument built to preserve the memory of the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brazilian_Declaration_of_Independence" title="Brazilian Declaration of Independence">
       Independence of Brazil
      </a>
      , opened on September 7, 1895, with the name of Museu de Cincias Naturais (Natural
      <a href="/wiki/Science_museum" title="Science museum">
       Science Museum
      </a>
      ). In 1919, it became a
      <a href="/wiki/History" title="History">
       history
      </a>
      museum. Reflecting the architectural influence of the Versailles Palace in France, the Ipiranga's collection, with approximately 100,000 pieces, comprises works of art, furniture, clothing and appliances that belonged to those who took part in
      <a href="/wiki/History_of_Brazil" title="History of Brazil">
       Brazilian history
      </a>
      , such as explorers, rulers and freedom fighters. Its facilities house a library with 100,000 books and the "Centro de Documentao Histrica," Historic Documentation Center, with 40,000
      <a href="/wiki/Manuscript" title="Manuscript">
       manuscripts
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      The
      <a href="/wiki/Ema_Gordon_Klabin_Cultural_Foundation" title="Ema Gordon Klabin Cultural Foundation">
       Ema Gordon Klabin Cultural Foundation
      </a>
      opened to the public in March 2007. Its headquarters is a 1920s mansion. It houses 1545 works, including paintings by
      <a href="/wiki/Marc_Chagall" title="Marc Chagall">
       Marc Chagall
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Pompeo_Batoni" title="Pompeo Batoni">
       Pompeo Batoni
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Pierre_Gobert" title="Pierre Gobert">
       Pierre Gobert
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Frans_Post" title="Frans Post">
       Frans Post
      </a>
      , Brazilian modernists
      <a href="/wiki/Tarsila_do_Amaral" title="Tarsila do Amaral">
       Tarsila do Amaral
      </a>
      ,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Di_Cavalcanti" title="Di Cavalcanti">
       Di Cavalcanti
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Candido_Portinari" title="Candido Portinari">
       Portinari
      </a>
      , period furniture, decorative and archaeological pieces.
     </p>
     <p>
      Stretching over 78,000 square meters,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Memorial_da_Am%C3%A9rica_Latina" title="Memorial da Amrica Latina">
       Memorial da Amrica Latina
      </a>
      (
      <i>
       Latin America's Memorial
      </i>
      ) was conceived to showcase
      <a href="/wiki/Latin_America" title="Latin America">
       Latin American countries
      </a>
      and their roots and cultures. It is home to the headquarters of Parlamento Latino-Americano Parlatino (Latin American Parliament). Designed by
      <a href="/wiki/Oscar_Niemeyer" title="Oscar Niemeyer">
       Oscar Niemeyer
      </a>
      , Memorial has an exhibition pavilion with permanent exhibition of the continent's craftwork production; a library with books, newspapers, magazines, videos, films and records about the history of Latin America; and an 1,679-seat auditorium.
     </p>
     <p>
      Hospedaria do Imigrante (
      <i>
       Immigrant's Hostel
      </i>
      ) was built in 1886 and opened in 1887. Immigrant's Hostel was built in Brs to welcome the immigrants who arrived in Brazil through the
      <a href="/wiki/Port_of_Santos" title="Port of Santos">
       Port of Santos
      </a>
      , quarantining those who were sick and helping new arrivals to find work in coffee plantations in Western, Northern and Southwestern So Paulo State and Northern Paran State. From 1882 to 1978, 2.5million immigrants of more than 60 nationalities and ethnicities were guests there,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hospedaria_dos_Imigrantes_1885_139-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Hospedaria_dos_Imigrantes_1885-139">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        139
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      all of them duly registered in the museum's books and lists. The hostel hosted approximately 3,000 people on average, but occasionally reached 8,000. The hostel received the last immigrants in 1978.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">
       <a href="#cite_note-140">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        140
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In 1998 the hostel became a museum, where it preserves the immigrants' documentation, memory and objects. Located in one of the few remaining centenarian buildings, the museum occupies part of the former hostel. The museum also restores wooden train wagons from the former
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Railway" title="So Paulo Railway">
       So Paulo Railway
      </a>
      . Two restored wagons inhabit the museum. One dates from 1914, while a second class passenger car dates from 1931. The museum records the names of all immigrants who were hosted there from 1888 to 1978.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">
       <a href="#cite_note-141">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        141
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Occupying an area of 700 square meters, the animals shown in the museum are samples of the country's tropical
      <a href="/wiki/Fauna" title="Fauna">
       fauna
      </a>
      and were prepared (embalmed) more than 50 years ago. The animals are grouped according to their classification: fish, amphibians, reptiles, birds and
      <a href="/wiki/Mammal" title="Mammal">
       mammals
      </a>
      and some invertebrates such as
      <a href="/wiki/Coral" title="Coral">
       corals
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Crustacean" title="Crustacean">
       crustaceans
      </a>
      and
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mollusk" title="Mollusk">
       mollusks
      </a>
      . The library specializes in
      <a href="/wiki/Zoology" title="Zoology">
       zoology
      </a>
      . It has 73,850 works, of which 8,473 are books and 2,364 are newspapers, in addition to theses and
      <a href="/wiki/Map" title="Map">
       maps
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Museum_of_Art" title="So Paulo Museum of Art">
       MASP
      </a>
      has one of world's most important collections of
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Western_art_history" title="Western art history">
       European art
      </a>
      . The most important collections cover Italian and French painting schools. The museum was founded by
      <a href="/wiki/Assis_Chateaubriand" title="Assis Chateaubriand">
       Assis Chateaubriand
      </a>
      and is directed by
      <a href="/wiki/Pietro_Maria_Bardi" title="Pietro Maria Bardi">
       Pietro Maria Bardi
      </a>
      . Its current headquarters, opened in 1968, were designed by
      <a href="/wiki/Lina_Bo_Bardi" title="Lina Bo Bardi">
       Lina Bo Bardi
      </a>
      . MASP organizes temporary exhibitions in special areas. Brazilian and international exhibitions of
      <a href="/wiki/Contemporary_art" title="Contemporary art">
       contemporary arts
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Photography" title="Photography">
       photography
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Design" title="Design">
       design
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Architecture" title="Architecture">
       architecture
      </a>
      take turn during the whole year.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142">
       <a href="#cite_note-142">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        142
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      The headquarters of the state government has a collection of works by Brazilian artists, such as
      <a href="/wiki/Candido_Portinari" title="Candido Portinari">
       Portinari
      </a>
      , Aldo Bonadei, Djanira,
      <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Ferraz_de_Almeida_J%C3%BAnior" title="Jos Ferraz de Almeida Jnior">
       Almeida Jnior
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Victor_Brecheret" title="Victor Brecheret">
       Victor Brecheret
      </a>
      , Ernesto de Fiori and
      <a href="/wiki/Aleijadinho" title="Aleijadinho">
       Aleijadinho
      </a>
      . It also gathers colonial furniture, leather and silver artefacts and European tapestry. In
      <a href="/wiki/Eclecticism_in_art" title="Eclecticism in art">
       eclectic style
      </a>
      , its walls are covered with panels describing the history of So Paulo.
     </p>
     <p>
      Located next to the Luz metro station, the building was projected by architect Ramos de Azevedo in 1895. It was constructed to house an Arts Lyceum. In 1911, it became the
      <a href="/wiki/Pinacoteca_do_Estado_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Pinacoteca do Estado de So Paulo">
       Pinacoteca do Estado de So Paulo
      </a>
      , where it currently hosts a number of art exhibitions. A major exhibition on the bronze statues of French sculptor
      <a href="/wiki/Auguste_Rodin" title="Auguste Rodin">
       Auguste Rodin
      </a>
      took place in 2001. There is also a permanent exhibition on the "Resistance" movement that took place during military dictatorship in the Republican period, including a reconstructed prison cell where political prisoners were kept.
     </p>
     <p>
      Also called Oca do Ibirapuera,
      <i>
       oca
      </i>
      means thatched house in Native Brazilian
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tupi-Guarani_languages" title="Tupi-Guarani languages">
       Tupi-Guarani
      </a>
      . A white, spaceship-like building sitting in the greens of Ibirapuera Park, Oca is an exhibition place with more than 10,000 squared metres. Modern art, Native Brazilian art, and photographies are some of the topics of past thematic exhibitions.
     </p>
     <p>
      <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Museum_of_Image_and_Sound" title="So Paulo Museum of Image and Sound">
       Museu da Imagem e do Som
      </a>
      (
      <i>
       Image and Sound Museum
      </i>
      ) preserves music, cinema, photography and
      <a href="/wiki/Graphic_design" title="Graphic design">
       graphical
      </a>
      arts. MIS has a collection of more than 200,000 images. It has more than 1,600 fiction videotapes, documentaries and music and 12,750 titles recorded in
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Super_8_mm_film" title="Super 8 mm film">
       Super 8
      </a>
      and 16mm film. MIS organizes concerts, cinema and video festivals and photography and graphical arts exhibitions.
     </p>
     <p>
      The
      <a href="/wiki/Museum_of_Art_of_the_Parliament_of_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="Museum of Art of the Parliament of So Paulo">
       Museum of Art of the Parliament of So Paulo
      </a>
      is a contemporary art museum housed in the Palcio 9 de Julho, the Legislative Assembly of So Paulo house. The museum is run by the Department of Artistic Heritage of the Legislative Assembly and has paintings, sculpture, prints, ceramics and photographs, exploring the Brazilian contemporary art.
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">
       Sports

       </span>
      </span>

      </a>

      <span class="mw-headline" id="Football">

      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">

       </a>

       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="thumb tright">

       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Est%C3%A1dio_Municipal_Paulo_Machado_de_Carvalho.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="598" data-file-width="900" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/Est%C3%A1dio_Municipal_Paulo_Machado_de_Carvalho.jpg/220px-Est%C3%A1dio_Municipal_Paulo_Machado_de_Carvalho.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/Est%C3%A1dio_Municipal_Paulo_Machado_de_Carvalho.jpg/330px-Est%C3%A1dio_Municipal_Paulo_Machado_de_Carvalho.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/Est%C3%A1dio_Municipal_Paulo_Machado_de_Carvalho.jpg/440px-Est%C3%A1dio_Municipal_Paulo_Machado_de_Carvalho.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Est%C3%A1dio_Municipal_Paulo_Machado_de_Carvalho.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Pacaembu_Stadium" title="Pacaembu Stadium">
         Pacaembu
        </a>
        , historic city stadium.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Allianz_Parque.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3598" data-file-width="4896" height="162" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Allianz_Parque.jpg/220px-Allianz_Parque.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Allianz_Parque.jpg/330px-Allianz_Parque.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Allianz_Parque.jpg/440px-Allianz_Parque.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Allianz_Parque.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Allianz_Parque" title="Allianz Parque">
         Allianz Parque
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="hatnote">
      See also:
      <a href="/wiki/Football_in_Brazil" title="Football in Brazil">
       Football in Brazil
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="Campeonato Brasileiro Srie A">
       Campeonato Brasileiro Srie A
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Paulista" title="Campeonato Paulista">
       Campeonato Paulista
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      As in the rest of Brazil,
      <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">
       football
      </a>
      is the most popular sport. The city's major teams are
      <a href="/wiki/Sport_Club_Corinthians_Paulista" title="Sport Club Corinthians Paulista">
       Corinthians
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Sociedade_Esportiva_Palmeiras" title="Sociedade Esportiva Palmeiras">
       Palmeiras
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_FC" title="So Paulo FC">
       So Paulo FC
      </a>
      .
      <a href="/wiki/Associa%C3%A7%C3%A3o_Portuguesa_de_Desportos" title="Associao Portuguesa de Desportos">
       Portuguesa
      </a>
      is a medium club and
      <a href="/wiki/Clube_Atl%C3%A9tico_Juventus" title="Clube Atltico Juventus">
       Juventus
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Nacional_Atl%C3%A9tico_Clube_(SP)" title="Nacional Atltico Clube (SP)">
       Nacional
      </a>
      are two small clubs.
     </p>
     <p>
      So Paulo was one of the host cities of the
      <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">
       2014 FIFA World Cup
      </a>
      , for which Brazil was the host nation. The
      <a href="/wiki/Arena_Corinthians" title="Arena Corinthians">
       Arena Corinthians
      </a>
      was built for the event and hosted six matches, including the opening.
     </p>

     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Brazilian_Grand_Prix">
       Brazilian Grand Prix
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=S%C3%A3o_Paulo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Brazilian Grand Prix">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">
      Main article:
      <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazilian Grand Prix
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">
       Formula One
      </a>
      is also one of the most popular sports in Brazil. Brazil's most famous sportsmen is perhaps three times Formula One world champion and So Paulo native
      <a href="/wiki/Ayrton_Senna" title="Ayrton Senna">
       Ayrton Senna
      </a>
      . The Formula One
      <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazilian Grand Prix
      </a>
      is held at the
      <a href="/wiki/Aut%C3%B3dromo_Jos%C3%A9_Carlos_Pace" title="Autdromo Jos Carlos Pace">
       Autdromo Jos Carlos Pace
      </a>
      in
      <a href="/wiki/Interlagos" title="Interlagos">
       Interlagos
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Socorro_(district_of_S%C3%A3o_Paulo)" title="Socorro (district of So Paulo)">
       Socorro
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      The Grand Prix has been held there from the inaugural in
      <a href="/wiki/1973_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1973 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       1973
      </a>
      until 1977, 19791980 and continuously since
      <a href="/wiki/1990_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1990 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       1990
      </a>
      . Four Brazilians have won the Brazilian Grand Prix in Interlagos (all of whom were/are So Paulo natives):
      <a href="/wiki/Emerson_Fittipaldi" title="Emerson Fittipaldi">
       Emerson Fittipaldi
      </a>
      (1973) and
      <a href="/wiki/1974_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1974 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       1974
      </a>
      ),
      <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Pace" title="Carlos Pace">
       Jos Carlos Pace
      </a>
      (
      <a href="/wiki/1975_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1975 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       1975
      </a>
      ),
      <a href="/wiki/Ayrton_Senna" title="Ayrton Senna">
       Ayrton Senna
      </a>
      (
      <a href="/wiki/1991_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1991 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       1991
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/1993_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1993 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       1993
      </a>
      ) and
      <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Massa" title="Felipe Massa">
       Felipe Massa
      </a>
      (
      <a href="/wiki/2006_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="2006 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       2006
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/2008_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="2008 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       2008
      </a>
      ).
     </p>
     <p>
      In
      <a href="/wiki/2007_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="2007 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       2007
      </a>
      , a new local railway station
      <i>
       Autdromo
      </i>
      of the Line C (Line 9) of
      <a href="/wiki/Companhia_Paulista_de_Trens_Metropolitanos" title="Companhia Paulista de Trens Metropolitanos">
       CPTM
      </a>
      , was constructed near the circuit to improve access.
     </p>
     <div class="thumb tnone" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right:auto; width:99%; max-width:908px;">
      <div class="thumbinner">
       <div class="overflowbugx" style="overflow:auto;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Interlagos_-big.jpg" title="Autdromo Jos Carlos Pace, the venue for the Brazilian Grand Prix.">
         <img alt="" data-file-height="2009" data-file-width="7876" height="230" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Interlagos_-big.jpg/900px-Interlagos_-big.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Interlagos_-big.jpg/1350px-Interlagos_-big.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dc/Interlagos_-big.jpg/1800px-Interlagos_-big.jpg 2x" width="900"/>
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a href="/wiki/File:Interlagos_-big.jpg" title="File:Interlagos -big.jpg">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Aut%C3%B3dromo_Jos%C3%A9_Carlos_Pace" title="Autdromo Jos Carlos Pace">
         Autdromo Jos Carlos Pace
        </a>
        , the venue for the
        <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="Brazilian Grand Prix">
         Brazilian Grand Prix
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Other_sports">
       Other sports
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=S%C3%A3o_Paulo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Other sports">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="thumb tleft">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Corrida_S%C3%A3o_Silvestre_2012.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="1536" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Corrida_S%C3%A3o_Silvestre_2012.jpg/220px-Corrida_S%C3%A3o_Silvestre_2012.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Corrida_S%C3%A3o_Silvestre_2012.jpg/330px-Corrida_S%C3%A3o_Silvestre_2012.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Corrida_S%C3%A3o_Silvestre_2012.jpg/440px-Corrida_S%C3%A3o_Silvestre_2012.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Corrida_S%C3%A3o_Silvestre_2012.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Saint_Silvester_Road_Race" title="Saint Silvester Road Race">
         Saint Silvester Road Race
        </a>
        in 2011
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      The
      <a href="/wiki/Saint_Silvester_Road_Race" title="Saint Silvester Road Race">
       So Silvestre
      </a>
      Race takes place every New Year's Eve. It was first held in 1925, when the competitors ran about 8,000 metres. Since then, the distance raced varied, but is now set at 15km (9.3mi).
     </p>
     <p>
      The
      <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Indy_300" title="So Paulo Indy 300">
       So Paulo Indy 300
      </a>
      was an
      <a href="/wiki/IndyCar_Series" title="IndyCar Series">
       IndyCar Series
      </a>
      race in
      <a href="/wiki/Santana_(district_of_S%C3%A3o_Paulo)" title="Santana (district of So Paulo)">
       Santana
      </a>
      that ran annually from 2010 to 2013. The event was removed from the
      <a href="/wiki/2014_IndyCar_Series_season" title="2014 IndyCar Series season">
       2014 season
      </a>
      calendar.
     </p>
     <p>
      Volleyball, basketball, skateboard and tennis are other major sports. There are several traditional
      <a href="/wiki/Sports_club" title="Sports club">
       sports clubs
      </a>
      in So Paulo that are home for teams in many championships. The most important are
      <a href="/wiki/Esporte_Clube_Pinheiros" title="Esporte Clube Pinheiros">
       Esporte Clube Pinheiros
      </a>
      (waterpolo,
      <a href="/wiki/Esporte_Clube_Pinheiros_(women%27s_volleyball)" title="Esporte Clube Pinheiros (women's volleyball)">
       women's volleyball
      </a>
      , swimming,
      <a href="/wiki/Esporte_Clube_Pinheiros_(basketball)" title="Esporte Clube Pinheiros (basketball)">
       men's basketball
      </a>
      and
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Team_handball" title="Team handball">
       handball
      </a>
      ),
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Clube_Athletico_Paulistano_(basketball)" title="Clube Athletico Paulistano (basketball)">
       Clube Athletico Paulistano (basketball)
      </a>
      , Esporte Clube Banespa (volleyball, handball and
      <a href="/wiki/Futsal" title="Futsal">
       futsal
      </a>
      ),
      <a href="/wiki/Esporte_Clube_S%C3%ADrio_(basketball)" title="Esporte Clube Srio (basketball)">
       Esporte Clube Srio (basketball)
      </a>
      , Associao Atltica Hebraica (basketball),
      <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Athletic_Club" title="So Paulo Athletic Club">
       So Paulo Athletic Club
      </a>
      (
      <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">
       rugby union
      </a>
      ), Pasteur Athltique Club (rugby union), Rio Branco Rugby Clube (rugby union), Bandeirantes Rugby Clube (rugby union), Clube de Regatas Tiet (multi-sports) and Clube Atltico Ipiranga (multi-sports and former professional football). Also, on Bom Retiro, there is a public baseball stadium, Estdio Mie Nishi.
     </p>
